#		#Western Sahara
		any_country = {
			limit = {
				FROM = { NOT = { has_country_flag = too_many_deliveries } }
				check_variable = { which = Dismantlement_Chair value = 0.99 }
				check_variable = { which = dismantlement_dollars value = 0.99 }
				NOT = { has_global_flag = Total_One_Victor }
				THIS = { tag = WSA }
			}
			FROM = {
				set_country_flag = too_many_deliveries
				random_owned = {
					limit = { owner = { THIS = { tag = WSA } } }
					owner = { THIS = { set_variable = { which = Western_Sahara_Colony value = 1 } } }
				}
			}
			THIS = { set_variable = { which = Colony_Event_Sent value = 1 } }
			country_event = 777771500
		}

#####		Colonial Dismantlement Leader Decision Events	620-629		#####

country_event = {
    id = 777770620
    title = "The $FROMCOUNTRY_ADJ$ Colony"
    desc = "EVTDESC777770620"
	picture = "dismantle 8"
    is_triggered_only = yes
	allow_multiple_instances = yes

	immediate = {
		any_country = {
			limit = {
				OR = { AND = { FROM = { OR = { government = democracy government = radical_republic government = prussian_constitutionalism government = hms_government government = constitutional_empire } } THIS = { OR = { government = democracy government = radical_republic government = prussian_constitutionalism government = hms_government government = constitutional_empire } } } AND = { FROM = { OR = { government = proletarian_dictatorship government = radical_republic government = prussian_constitutionalism } } THIS = { OR = { government = proletarian_dictatorship } } } AND = { FROM = { OR = { government = presidential_dictatorship government = fascist_dictatorship } } THIS = { OR = { government = presidential_dictatorship government = fascist_dictatorship } } } AND = { FROM = { OR = { government = absolute_monarchy government = absolute_empire government = semi_constitutional_empire } } THIS = { OR = { government = absolute_monarchy government = absolute_empire government = semi_constitutional_empire } } } }
			}
			THIS = { set_country_flag = common_government_bonus }
		}
		any_country = {
			limit = {

		}

    }

        name = "We shall take them for ourselves."

				tag = FROM
			}
			set_variable = { which = Annex_Colony value = 1 }
			country_event = 777770630
        }
		change_variable = {
            which = dismantlement_dollars
            value = -1
        }
        set_country_flag = dismantlement_dollars_target badboy = 1
        CLN = { country_event = 777771700 }
        ai_chance = {
            factor = 4
			modifier = { factor = 0.5 has_country_flag = we_control_core_penalty }
			modifier = { factor = 15 badboy = 23 }
			modifier = { factor = 1 badboy = 17 }
			modifier = { factor = 2 has_country_flag = monarchy_government }
        }
    }
    option = {
        name = "We shall offer $FROMCOUNTRY$ to other victors."
        any_country = {
			limit = {
				tag = FROM
			}
			set_variable = { which = Give_Away_Colony value = 1 }
			country_event = 777770630
        }
        ai_chance = {
            factor = 4
			modifier = { factor = 0.5 has_country_flag = we_control_core_penalty }
			modifier = { factor = 15 badboy = 23 }
			modifier = { factor = 1 badboy = 17 }
			modifier = { factor = 1 has_country_flag = monarchy_government }
        }
    }
    option = {

				tag = FROM
			}
			set_variable = { which = As_Is_Colony value = 1 }

				truce_with = THIS
			}
			THIS = { set_country_flag = truce_with_this_penalty }
		}
		set_country_flag = annex_overwrite
    }

			owner = { UTI = { all_core = { remove_core = UTI } } }
		}
		random_owned = {
			limit = { owner = { NOT = { any_owned_province = { NOT = { is_core = UTI } } } check_variable = { which = Annex_Colony value = 0.99 } } }
			owner = { annex_to = UTI UTI = { all_core = { remove_core = UTI } } }
		}
		random_owned = {
			limit = { owner = { any_owned_province = { NOT = { is_core = UTI } } check_variable = { which = Annex_Colony value = 0.99 } } }
			owner = {
				any_owned = { limit = { is_core = UTI is_core = THIS } remove_core = THIS add_core = CLN }
				release = UTI
				UTI = { annex_to = UTI any_owned = { limit = { is_core = CLN } add_core = THIS remove_core = CLN } all_core = { remove_core = UTI } }
			}
		}

			}

		}

		UTI = { all_core = { remove_core = UTI } }

		THIS = { set_variable = { which = Outcome_Required value = 0 } }
    }
}

			}
			THIS = { set_country_flag = common_government_bonus }
		}
		any_country = {
			limit = {
				OR = { AND = { FROM = { OR = { government = democracy government = radical_republic government = prussian_constitutionalism government = hms_government government = constitutional_empire } } THIS = { OR = { government = democracy government = radical_republic government = prussian_constitutionalism government = hms_government government = constitutional_empire } } } AND = { FROM = { OR = { government = proletarian_dictatorship government = radical_republic government = prussian_constitutionalism } } THIS = { OR = { government = proletarian_dictatorship } } } AND = { FROM = { OR = { government = presidential_dictatorship government = fascist_dictatorship } } THIS = { OR = { government = presidential_dictatorship government = fascist_dictatorship } } } AND = { FROM = { OR = { government = absolute_monarchy government = absolute_empire government = semi_constitutional_empire } } THIS = { OR = { government = absolute_monarchy government = absolute_empire government = semi_constitutional_empire } } } }
			}
			THIS = { set_country_flag = conflicting_government_penalty }
		}
		any_country = {
			limit = {
				tag = FROM
				badboy = 0.8
			}
			THIS = { set_country_flag = infamous_penalty }
		}
		any_country = {
			limit = {
				tag = FROM
				any_core = { owned_by = THIS }
			}
			THIS = { set_country_flag = we_control_core_penalty }
		}
		any_country = {

				tag = FROM
				OR = {
					has_country_modifier = recently_lost_war

					military_access = THIS
				}

			THIS = { set_country_flag = recent_state_bonus }

			}
			THIS = { set_country_flag = holdout_slavery_bonus }
		}

				truce_with = THIS
			}
			THIS = { set_country_flag = truce_with_this_penalty }
		}
		set_country_flag = annex_overwrite
    }

    option = {
        name = "We shall take them for ourselves."
		change_variable = {
            which = dismantlement_dollars
            value = -1
        }
        set_country_flag = dismantlement_dollars_target badboy = 1

country_event = {
    id = 777771514
    title = "The $FROMCOUNTRY_ADJ$ Colony"
    desc = "EVTDESC777771514"
	picture = "dismantle 15"
    is_triggered_only = yes
	allow_multiple_instances = yes

	immediate = {
		any_country = {
			limit = {
				OR = { AND = { FROM = { OR = { government = democracy government = radical_republic government = prussian_constitutionalism government = hms_government government = constitutional_empire } } THIS = { OR = { government = democracy government = radical_republic government = prussian_constitutionalism government = hms_government government = constitutional_empire } } } AND = { FROM = { OR = { government = proletarian_dictatorship government = radical_republic government = prussian_constitutionalism } } THIS = { OR = { government = proletarian_dictatorship } } } AND = { FROM = { OR = { government = presidential_dictatorship government = fascist_dictatorship } } THIS = { OR = { government = presidential_dictatorship government = fascist_dictatorship } } } AND = { FROM = { OR = { government = absolute_monarchy government = absolute_empire government = semi_constitutional_empire } } THIS = { OR = { government = absolute_monarchy government = absolute_empire government = semi_constitutional_empire } } } }
			}
			THIS = { set_country_flag = common_government_bonus }
		}
		any_country = {
			limit = {
				OR = { AND = { FROM = { OR = { government = democracy government = radical_republic government = prussian_constitutionalism government = hms_government government = constitutional_empire } } THIS = { OR = { government = democracy government = radical_republic government = prussian_constitutionalism government = hms_government government = constitutional_empire } } } AND = { FROM = { OR = { government = proletarian_dictatorship government = radical_republic government = prussian_constitutionalism } } THIS = { OR = { government = proletarian_dictatorship } } } AND = { FROM = { OR = { government = presidential_dictatorship government = fascist_dictatorship } } THIS = { OR = { government = presidential_dictatorship government = fascist_dictatorship } } } AND = { FROM = { OR = { government = absolute_monarchy government = absolute_empire government = semi_constitutional_empire } } THIS = { OR = { government = absolute_monarchy government = absolute_empire government = semi_constitutional_empire } } } }
			}
			THIS = { set_country_flag = conflicting_government_penalty }
		}
		any_country = {
			limit = {
				tag = FROM
				badboy = 0.8
			}
			THIS = { set_country_flag = infamous_penalty }
		}
		any_country = {
			limit = {
				tag = FROM
				any_core = { owned_by = THIS }
			}
			THIS = { set_country_flag = we_control_core_penalty }
		}
		any_country = {
			limit = {
				tag = FROM
				OR = {
					has_country_modifier = recently_lost_war
					is_disarmed = yes
					military_access = THIS
				}
			}
			THIS = { set_country_flag = recent_state_bonus }
		}
		any_country = {
			limit = {
				tag = FROM
				FROM = { slavery = yes_slavery }
				THIS = { slavery = yes_slavery }
			}
			THIS = { set_country_flag = holdout_slavery_bonus }
		}
		any_country = {
			limit = {
				tag = FROM
				truce_with = THIS
			}
			THIS = { set_country_flag = truce_with_this_penalty }
		}
		set_country_flag = annex_overwrite
    }

    option = {
        name = "We shall take them for ourselves."
		change_variable = {
            which = dismantlement_dollars
            value = -1
        }
        set_country_flag = dismantlement_dollars_target badboy = 1
        CLN = { country_event = 777771700 }
        any_country = {
			limit = {
				tag = FROM
			}
			set_variable = { which = Annex_Colony value = 1 }
			country_event = 777770630
        }
		ai_chance = {
            factor = 4
			modifier = { factor = 0.5 has_country_flag = we_control_core_penalty }
			modifier = { factor = 15 badboy = 23 }
			modifier = { factor = 2 badboy = 17 }
			modifier = { factor = 3 has_country_flag = monarchy_government }
        }
    }
    option = {

			limit = {
				tag = FROM
			}
			set_variable = { which = Give_Away_Colony value = 1 }

			}

		}

    }

country_event = {
    id = 777771519
    title = "The $FROMCOUNTRY_ADJ$ Colony"
    desc = "EVTDESC777771519"
	picture = "dismantle 21"
    is_triggered_only = yes
	allow_multiple_instances = yes

	immediate = {
		any_country = {
			limit = {
				OR = { AND = { FROM = { OR = { government = democracy government = radical_republic government = prussian_constitutionalism government = hms_government government = constitutional_empire } } THIS = { OR = { government = democracy government = radical_republic government = prussian_constitutionalism government = hms_government government = constitutional_empire } } } AND = { FROM = { OR = { government = proletarian_dictatorship government = radical_republic government = prussian_constitutionalism } } THIS = { OR = { government = proletarian_dictatorship } } } AND = { FROM = { OR = { government = presidential_dictatorship government = fascist_dictatorship } } THIS = { OR = { government = presidential_dictatorship government = fascist_dictatorship } } } AND = { FROM = { OR = { government = absolute_monarchy government = absolute_empire government = semi_constitutional_empire } } THIS = { OR = { government = absolute_monarchy government = absolute_empire government = semi_constitutional_empire } } } }
			}
			THIS = { set_country_flag = common_government_bonus }
		}
		any_country = {
			limit = {
				OR = { AND = { FROM = { OR = { government = democracy government = radical_republic government = prussian_constitutionalism government = hms_government government = constitutional_empire } } THIS = { OR = { government = democracy government = radical_republic government = prussian_constitutionalism government = hms_government government = constitutional_empire } } } AND = { FROM = { OR = { government = proletarian_dictatorship government = radical_republic government = prussian_constitutionalism } } THIS = { OR = { government = proletarian_dictatorship } } } AND = { FROM = { OR = { government = presidential_dictatorship government = fascist_dictatorship } } THIS = { OR = { government = presidential_dictatorship government = fascist_dictatorship } } } AND = { FROM = { OR = { government = absolute_monarchy government = absolute_empire government = semi_constitutional_empire } } THIS = { OR = { government = absolute_monarchy government = absolute_empire government = semi_constitutional_empire } } } }
			}
			THIS = { set_country_flag = conflicting_government_penalty }
		}
		any_country = {
			limit = {
				tag = FROM
				badboy = 0.8
			}
			THIS = { set_country_flag = infamous_penalty }
		}
		any_country = {
			limit = {
				tag = FROM
				any_core = { owned_by = THIS }
			}
			THIS = { set_country_flag = we_control_core_penalty }
		}
		any_country = {
			limit = {
				tag = FROM
				OR = {
					has_country_modifier = recently_lost_war
					is_disarmed = yes
					military_access = THIS
				}
			}
			THIS = { set_country_flag = recent_state_bonus }
		}
		any_country = {
			limit = {
				tag = FROM
				FROM = { slavery = yes_slavery }
				THIS = { slavery = yes_slavery }
			}
			THIS = { set_country_flag = holdout_slavery_bonus }
		}
		any_country = {
			limit = {
				tag = FROM
				truce_with = THIS
			}
			THIS = { set_country_flag = truce_with_this_penalty }
		}
		set_country_flag = annex_overwrite
    }

    option = {
        name = "We shall take them for ourselves."
		change_variable = {
            which = dismantlement_dollars
            value = -1
        }
        set_country_flag = dismantlement_dollars_target badboy = 1
        CLN = { country_event = 777771700 }
        any_country = {
			limit = {
				tag = FROM
			}
			set_variable = { which = Annex_Colony value = 1 }
			country_event = 777770630
        }
		ai_chance = {
            factor = 4
			modifier = { factor = 0.5 has_country_flag = we_control_core_penalty }
			modifier = { factor = 15 badboy = 23 }
			modifier = { factor = 2 badboy = 17 }
			modifier = { factor = 3 has_country_flag = monarchy_government }
        }
    }
    option = {
        name = "We shall offer $FROMCOUNTRY$ to other victors."
        any_country = {
			limit = {
				tag = FROM
			}
			set_variable = { which = Give_Away_Colony value = 1 }
			country_event = 777770630
        }
        ai_chance = {
            factor = 4
			modifier = { factor = 0.5 has_country_flag = we_control_core_penalty }
			modifier = { factor = 15 badboy = 23 }
			modifier = { factor = 2 badboy = 17 }
			modifier = { factor = 2 has_country_flag = monarchy_government }
        }
    }
    option = {
        name = "They shall remain with the defeated."
        any_country = {
			limit = {
				tag = FROM
			}
			set_variable = { which = As_Is_Colony value = 1 }
			country_event = 777770630
        }
        ai_chance = {
            factor = 1
			modifier = { factor = 2 has_country_flag = infamous_penalty }
			modifier = { factor = 3 has_country_flag = we_control_core_penalty }
			modifier = { factor = 0.5 has_country_flag = truce_with_this_penalty }
			modifier = { factor = 15 badboy = 23 }
			modifier = { factor = 2 badboy = 17 }
        }
    }
    option = {
        name = "They shall exist as an independent state."
        any_country = {
			limit = {
				tag = FROM
			}
			set_variable = { which = Independent_Colony value = 1 }
			country_event = 777770630
        }
        ai_chance = {
            factor = 2
			modifier = { factor = 15 OR = { government = democracy government = proletarian_dictatorship } }
			modifier = { factor = 2 relation = { who = FROM value = 120 } }
			modifier = { factor = 2 trade_policy = free_trade }
			modifier = { factor = 2 has_country_flag = recent_state_bonus }
			modifier = { factor = 0.5 has_country_flag = we_control_core_penalty }
			modifier = { factor = 0.05 badboy = 23 }
			modifier = { factor = 0.75 badboy = 17 }
        }

			limit = {
				tag = FROM

			set_variable = { which = Integrate_Colony value = 1 }
			country_event = 777770630
        }
        ai_chance = {
            factor = 2
			modifier = { factor = 15 OR = { government = democracy government = proletarian_dictatorship } }
			modifier = { factor = 2 relation = { who = FROM value = 120 } }
			modifier = { factor = 2 trade_policy = free_trade }
			modifier = { factor = 2 has_country_flag = recent_state_bonus }
			modifier = { factor = 0.5 has_country_flag = we_control_core_penalty }

	allow_multiple_instances = yes

	immediate = {

			}
			THIS = { set_country_flag = common_government_bonus }
		}
		any_country = {
			limit = {
				OR = { AND = { FROM = { OR = { government = democracy government = radical_republic government = prussian_constitutionalism government = hms_government government = constitutional_empire } } THIS = { OR = { government = democracy government = radical_republic government = prussian_constitutionalism government = hms_government government = constitutional_empire } } } AND = { FROM = { OR = { government = proletarian_dictatorship government = radical_republic government = prussian_constitutionalism } } THIS = { OR = { government = proletarian_dictatorship } } } AND = { FROM = { OR = { government = presidential_dictatorship government = fascist_dictatorship } } THIS = { OR = { government = presidential_dictatorship government = fascist_dictatorship } } } AND = { FROM = { OR = { government = absolute_monarchy government = absolute_empire government = semi_constitutional_empire } } THIS = { OR = { government = absolute_monarchy government = absolute_empire government = semi_constitutional_empire } } } }
			}

		}

				tag = FROM
				any_core = { owned_by = THIS }
			}
			THIS = { set_country_flag = we_control_core_penalty }
		}
		any_country = {
			limit = {
				tag = FROM
				OR = {
					has_country_modifier = recently_lost_war
					is_disarmed = yes
					military_access = THIS
				}
			}
			THIS = { set_country_flag = recent_state_bonus }
		}
		any_country = {
			limit = {
				tag = FROM

				THIS = { slavery = yes_slavery }
			}
			THIS = { set_country_flag = holdout_slavery_bonus }
		}
		any_country = {
			limit = {
				tag = FROM
				truce_with = THIS
			}
			THIS = { set_country_flag = truce_with_this_penalty }
		}
		set_country_flag = annex_overwrite
    }

    option = {
        name = "We shall take them for ourselves."
		change_variable = {

		}
		any_country = {

				OR = { AND = { FROM = { OR = { government = democracy government = radical_republic government = prussian_constitutionalism government = hms_government government = constitutional_empire } } THIS = { OR = { government = democracy government = radical_republic government = prussian_constitutionalism government = hms_government government = constitutional_empire } } } AND = { FROM = { OR = { government = proletarian_dictatorship government = radical_republic government = prussian_constitutionalism } } THIS = { OR = { government = proletarian_dictatorship } } } AND = { FROM = { OR = { government = presidential_dictatorship government = fascist_dictatorship } } THIS = { OR = { government = presidential_dictatorship government = fascist_dictatorship } } } AND = { FROM = { OR = { government = absolute_monarchy government = absolute_empire government = semi_constitutional_empire } } THIS = { OR = { government = absolute_monarchy government = absolute_empire government = semi_constitutional_empire } } } }

				tag = FROM

			}
			THIS = { set_country_flag = we_control_core_penalty }
		}
		any_country = {
			limit = {
				tag = FROM
				OR = {
					has_country_modifier = recently_lost_war
					is_disarmed = yes
					military_access = THIS
				}
			}
			THIS = { set_country_flag = recent_state_bonus }

				THIS = { slavery = yes_slavery }
			}
			THIS = { set_country_flag = holdout_slavery_bonus }
		}
		any_country = {
			limit = {
				tag = FROM
				truce_with = THIS
			}
			THIS = { set_country_flag = truce_with_this_penalty }
		}
		set_country_flag = annex_overwrite
    }

			}

		}
		any_country = {

				OR = { AND = { FROM = { OR = { government = democracy government = radical_republic government = prussian_constitutionalism government = hms_government government = constitutional_empire } } THIS = { OR = { government = democracy government = radical_republic government = prussian_constitutionalism government = hms_government government = constitutional_empire } } } AND = { FROM = { OR = { government = proletarian_dictatorship government = radical_republic government = prussian_constitutionalism } } THIS = { OR = { government = proletarian_dictatorship } } } AND = { FROM = { OR = { government = presidential_dictatorship government = fascist_dictatorship } } THIS = { OR = { government = presidential_dictatorship government = fascist_dictatorship } } } AND = { FROM = { OR = { government = absolute_monarchy government = absolute_empire government = semi_constitutional_empire } } THIS = { OR = { government = absolute_monarchy government = absolute_empire government = semi_constitutional_empire } } } }
			}

			}
			THIS = { set_country_flag = we_control_core_penalty }

				truce_with = THIS
			}
			THIS = { set_country_flag = truce_with_this_penalty }
		}
		set_country_flag = annex_overwrite
    }

		}

					is_disarmed = yes
					military_access = THIS
				}
			}
			THIS = { set_country_flag = recent_state_bonus }
		}
		any_country = {
			limit = {
				tag = FROM
				FROM = { slavery = yes_slavery }
				THIS = { slavery = yes_slavery }
			}
			THIS = { set_country_flag = holdout_slavery_bonus }
		}
		any_country = {
			limit = {
				tag = FROM
				truce_with = THIS
			}
			THIS = { set_country_flag = truce_with_this_penalty }
		}
		set_country_flag = annex_overwrite
    }

    option = {
        name = "They shall remain with the defeated."
        any_country = {
			limit = {
				tag = FROM
			}
			set_variable = { which = As_Is_Colony value = 1 }
			country_event = 777770630
        }
        ai_chance = {
            factor = 1
			modifier = { factor = 2 has_country_flag = infamous_penalty }
			modifier = { factor = 3 has_country_flag = we_control_core_penalty }
			modifier = { factor = 0.5 has_country_flag = truce_with_this_penalty }
			modifier = { factor = 15 badboy = 23 }
			modifier = { factor = 2 badboy = 17 }
        }
    }
    option = {
        name = "They shall exist as an independent state."
        any_country = {
			limit = {
				tag = FROM
			}
			set_variable = { which = Independent_Colony value = 1 }
			country_event = 777770630
        }
        ai_chance = {
            factor = 2
			modifier = { factor = 15 OR = { government = democracy government = proletarian_dictatorship } }
			modifier = { factor = 2 relation = { who = FROM value = 120 } }
			modifier = { factor = 2 trade_policy = free_trade }
			modifier = { factor = 2 has_country_flag = recent_state_bonus }
			modifier = { factor = 0.5 has_country_flag = we_control_core_penalty }
			modifier = { factor = 0.05 badboy = 23 }
			modifier = { factor = 0.75 badboy = 17 }
        }
    }

	option = {
        name = "Integrate $FROMCOUNTRY$ into India"
        any_country = {
			limit = {
				tag = FROM
			}
			set_variable = { which = Integrate_Colony value = 1 }
			set_variable = { which = Kashmir_India value = 1 }
			country_event = 777770630
        }
        ai_chance = {
            factor = 2

			modifier = { factor = 2 relation = { who = FROM value = 120 } }

			modifier = { factor = 2 has_country_flag = recent_state_bonus }
			modifier = { factor = 0.5 has_country_flag = we_control_core_penalty }
			modifier = { factor = 0.05 badboy = 23 }
			modifier = { factor = 0.75 badboy = 17 }
        }
    }

	option = {
        name = "Integrate $FROMCOUNTRY$ into Pakistan"
        any_country = {
			limit = {
				tag = FROM
			}
			set_variable = { which = Integrate_Colony value = 1 }
			set_variable = { which = Kashmir_Pakistan value = 1 }
			country_event = 777770630
        }
        ai_chance = {
            factor = 2
			modifier = { factor = 15 OR = { government = democracy government = proletarian_dictatorship } }
			modifier = { factor = 2 relation = { who = FROM value = 120 } }
			modifier = { factor = 2 trade_policy = free_trade }
			modifier = { factor = 2 has_country_flag = recent_state_bonus }
			modifier = { factor = 0.5 has_country_flag = we_control_core_penalty }
			modifier = { factor = 0.05 badboy = 23 }
			modifier = { factor = 0.75 badboy = 17 }
        }
    }

	option = {
        name = "Split it between India and Pakistan"
        any_country = {
			limit = {
				tag = FROM
			}
			set_variable = { which = Integrate_Colony value = 1 }
			set_variable = { which = Kashmir_Split value = 1 }
			country_event = 777770630
        }
        ai_chance = {
            factor = 2

			modifier = { factor = 2 relation = { who = FROM value = 120 } }

country_event = {
    id = 777771571
    title = "The $FROMCOUNTRY_ADJ$ Colony"
    desc = "EVTDESC777771571"
	picture = "dismantle 21"
    is_triggered_only = yes
	allow_multiple_instances = yes

	immediate = {
		any_country = {
			limit = {
				OR = { AND = { FROM = { OR = { government = democracy government = radical_republic government = prussian_constitutionalism government = hms_government government = constitutional_empire } } THIS = { OR = { government = democracy government = radical_republic government = prussian_constitutionalism government = hms_government government = constitutional_empire } } } AND = { FROM = { OR = { government = proletarian_dictatorship government = radical_republic government = prussian_constitutionalism } } THIS = { OR = { government = proletarian_dictatorship } } } AND = { FROM = { OR = { government = presidential_dictatorship government = fascist_dictatorship } } THIS = { OR = { government = presidential_dictatorship government = fascist_dictatorship } } } AND = { FROM = { OR = { government = absolute_monarchy government = absolute_empire government = semi_constitutional_empire } } THIS = { OR = { government = absolute_monarchy government = absolute_empire government = semi_constitutional_empire } } } }

				}

				THIS = { slavery = yes_slavery }
			}
			THIS = { set_country_flag = holdout_slavery_bonus }

				tag = FROM
				truce_with = THIS
			}
			THIS = { set_country_flag = truce_with_this_penalty }
		}
		set_country_flag = annex_overwrite
    }
